msg:If you are looking for a quiet hotel in the area well connected to the train station, this is it. 

Everyone in the hotel were genuinely friendly and helpful. Room was clean and specious, although if you are a non smoker better inform the hotel to prepare a room without the cigarette smell. 

They have Chinese style breakfast. During the weekdays, with only few guest, there weren't much choice, but everything was good. During weekends with more guests there were a lot of options. Only if they have real coffee, not instant...

Hot Springs Area was additionally paid 88 per person, open 14-21. It was a very nice experience, but expect a lot of people during weekends. Unfortunately while inside, you cannot to go to the hotel restaurant to eat something, but you can order waimai.

Overall we had a very pleasant stay and big thanks to the front desk staff for all the support ğŸ˜Š

msg:This so-called hot spring resort is really scary! We arrived at 4pm on a weekday and were told that the outdoor hot springs would only start to heat up at 7pm! At night, about half of the outdoor "Dragon Palace" did not have hot spring water turned on. As for the tourists using the hot springs, they had Chinese characteristics. Some kept smoking in the hot spring water, some took pictures with their mobile phones, and some took several boxes of food. Eating and shouting in the pool...
The hot spring water in the hotel room is not warm at all. You have to inform the front desk after 10 a.m. before the staff can empty it from the hotel's hot spring reservoir and transport it to the "spring water" one kilometer away. For house use.
You have to wash the layers of dust in the bathtub in the room yourself!
If you want to experience an amazing hot spring vacation, this is the place to go.
In addition, the hot spring is an hour's drive from Paifang Street in the city. There are no restaurants nearby, and there is no hotel transfer to or from the station or the city.
Finally, I would like to thank all the front desk staff. The above mentioned is not your fault. Your work attitude is great! #ä¸­volt
